void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;

    u_xlat2 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1];
